{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01BtVLcA1R39yU7jGk581Asa","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n     2→// Copyright Authors of Cilium\n     3→\n     4→package resource\n     5→\n     6→import (\n     7→\t\"context\"\n     8→\t\"fmt\"\n     9→\t\"reflect\"\n    10→\t\"runtime\"\n    11→\t\"strconv\"\n    12→\t\"strings\"\n    13→\t\"sync\"\n    14→\n    15→\t\"github.com/cilium/hive/cell\"\n    16→\t\"github.com/cilium/stream\"\n    17→\tcorev1 \"k8s.io/api/core/v1\"\n    18→\t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/meta\"\n    19→\tk8sRuntime \"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime\"\n    20→\t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types\"\n    21→\t\"k8s.io/client-go/tools/cache\"\n    22→\t\"k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue\"\n    23→\t\"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client/apiutil\"\n    24→\n    25→\tk8smetrics \"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/metrics\"\n    26→\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/synced\"\n    27→\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/watchers/resources\"\n    28→\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n    29→\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/metrics\"\n    30→\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/promise\"\n    31→)\n    32→\n    33→// Resource provides access to a Kubernetes resource through either\n    34→// a stream of events or a read-only store.\n    35→//\n    36→// Observing of the events can be done from a constructor as subscriber\n    37→// registration is non-blocking.\n    38→//\n    39→// Store() however should only be called from a start hook, or from a\n    40→// goroutine forked from the start hook as it blocks until the store\n    41→// has been synchronized.\n    42→//\n    43→// The subscriber can process the events from Events() asynchronously and in\n    44→// parallel, but for each event the Done() function must be called to mark\n    45→// the event as handled. If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\n    46→// If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\n    47→// (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\n    48→// later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\n    49→// WithRateLimiter option to Events().\n    50→//\n    51→// The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\n    52→// has been made to Events() or Store().\n    53→type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n    54→\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\n    55→\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\n    56→\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\n    57→\n    58→\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\n    59→\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\n    60→\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\n    61→\t//\n    62→\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\n    63→\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\n    64→\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\n    65→\t//\n    66→\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\n    67→\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\n    68→\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\n    69→\t// updates:\n    70→\t//\n    71→\t//\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\n    72→\t//\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n    73→\t//\n    74→\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\n    75→\t// all been marked Done() without an error.
